● Here's my proposal:

  Process: Surface-check every standalone DROP in drop_new.txt

  For each branch, do ONE targeted verification command against master — not a full re-investigation, just confirming the specific evidence claim from the log is true.
  The check depends on the drop reason:

  1. "Already upstream" with a specific master line/symbol — grep for that exact symbol/string on master. If found → confirmed. If not found → flag for re-investigation.
  2. "ALREADY_APPLIED" (branch tip = master tip) — verify git show --no-patch --format='%s' BRANCH returns kern/misc: Restore grub_memcpy() (the master tip subject). If
  yes → confirmed. If different subject → flag.
  3. "Superseded by vN" — verify the superseding branch exists in a KEEP series or is itself upstream. One check.
  4. "Grouped with X" — verify branch X is itself confirmed.

  Process 5 at a time, sequentially. No batching of the verification step itself — each check runs individually so a failure is immediately visible.

  Does this work?

──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   # Check 1: Every branch marked "KEEP" in the logs should be in standalone.txt or series/
   # Check 2: Every branch marked "DROP" in the logs should be in drop_new.txt                                                                              
   # Check 3: No branch should be marked KEEP in one log and DROP in the other

   # Extract all KEEP/DROP decisions from both logs
   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re, os

   def extract_decisions(filename):
       decisions = {}
       current_branches = []
       current_decision = None

       for line in open(filename):
           # Match heading with decision
           m = re.match(r'^## .*(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}).*— (DROP|KEEP)', line)
           if m:
               current_decision = m.group(2)
               # Extract ALL branch IDs from the heading line
               current_branches = re.findall(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', line)
               for b in current_branches:
                   decisions[b] = current_decision

           # Match branch IDs in table rows with verdicts
           tm = re.match(r'^\| (20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}) \|.*\| (Already upstream|Not upstream|.*upstream.*) \|', line)
           if tm:
               b = tm.group(1)
               verdict = tm.group(2)
               if 'Not upstream' in verdict:
                   decisions[b] = 'KEEP'
               elif 'Already upstream' in verdict or 'upstream' in verdict.lower():
                   decisions[b] = 'DROP'

           # Match "Dropped branches:" lines
           dm = re.match(r'^\*\*Dropped branches\*\*: (.+)', line)
           if dm:
               for b in re.findall(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', dm.group(1)):
                   decisions[b] = 'DROP'

           # Match "Kept branches:" lines
           km = re.match(r'^\*\*Kept branches\*\*: (.+)', line)
           if km:
               for b in re.findall(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', km.group(1)):
                   decisions[b] = 'KEEP'

       return decisions

   series_dec = extract_decisions('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
   standalone_dec = extract_decisions('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')

   # Ground truth
   drops = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/drop_new.txt'))
   standalone_keep = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/standalone.txt'))
   series_keep = set()
   for sf in os.listdir('import/series'):
       for line in open(f'import/series/{sf}'):
           series_keep.add(line.strip())
   all_keep = standalone_keep | series_keep

   # Merge log decisions
   all_dec = {}
   all_dec.update(series_dec)
   all_dec.update(standalone_dec)

   # Check: branches logged as KEEP but actually in drops
   wrong_keep = []
   for b, dec in all_dec.items():
       if dec == 'KEEP' and b in drops:
           wrong_keep.append(b)

   # Check: branches logged as DROP but actually in keeps
   wrong_drop = []
   for b, dec in all_dec.items():
       if dec == 'DROP' and b in all_keep:
           wrong_drop.append(b)

   # Check: branches in keeps with no log decision
   keep_no_log = sorted(all_keep - set(all_dec.keys()))

   # Check: branches in drops with no log decision
   drop_no_log = sorted(drops - set(all_dec.keys()))

   print(f"=== LOG vs REALITY ===")
   print(f"Logged as KEEP but in drop_new.txt: {len(wrong_keep)}")
   for b in sorted(wrong_keep):
       src = "series_log" if b in series_dec else "standalone_log"
       print(f"  {b} [{src}]")

   print(f"\nLogged as DROP but in keep lists: {len(wrong_drop)}")
   for b in sorted(wrong_drop):
       print(f"  {b}")

   print(f"\nIn keep lists but no log decision: {len(keep_no_log)}")
   for b in keep_no_log:
       print(f"  {b}")

   print(f"\nIn drop_new.txt but no log decision: {len(drop_no_log)}")
   for b in drop_no_log[:10]:
       print(f"  {b}")
   if len(drop_no_log) > 10:
       print(f"  ... and {len(drop_no_log) - 10} more")

 Bash command

   # Clean approach: get unique series heads from unconfirmed drops by matching
   # the first 2 fields (YYYY-MM) + checking which log entries they belong to
   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re

   unconfirmed = set(l.strip() for l in open('/tmp/unconfirmed_series_drops.txt'))

   # Parse log to find series -> members mapping for DROP series
   series_heads = []
   current_head = None
   current_members = []
   is_drop = False

   for line in open('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md'):
       m = re.match(r'^## Series: (20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', line)
       if m:
           if current_head and is_drop:
               series_heads.append((current_head, current_members))
           current_head = m.group(1)
           current_members = []
           is_drop = False

       # Collect branch IDs from table rows and Dropped branches lines
       for bm in re.finditer(r'\b(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})\b', line):
           b = bm.group(1)
           if b in unconfirmed and b not in current_members:
               current_members.append(b)

       if 'Decision' in line and 'DROP' in line:
           is_drop = True
       if 'Dropped branches' in line:
  ⎿  2 skills available

   import re

   def find_branches_in_file(filename):
       """Return set of all branch IDs mentioned in the file."""
       branches = set()
       for line in open(filename):
           for m in re.finditer(r'\b(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})\b', line):
               branches.add(m.group(1))
       return branches

   standalone_log = find_branches_in_file('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')
   series_log = find_branches_in_file('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')

   # Standalone confirmed drops
   confirmed = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/confirmed.txt'))
   # Series confirmed heads
   confirmed_series = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/confirmed_series.txt'))

   # Also get all series member branches for the confirmed series
   # (they should be in INSPECTION_LOG.md, not standalone)
   drops = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/drop_new.txt'))
   series_members = drops - confirmed  # 122 branches belonging to confirmed series

   print("=== STANDALONE CONFIRMED (confirmed.txt) ===")
   print(f"Total: {len(confirmed)}")

   only_standalone = 0
   only_series = 0
   in_both = 0
   in_neither = 0

   for b in sorted(confirmed):
       in_s = b in standalone_log
       in_r = b in series_log
       if in_s and in_r:
           in_both += 1
       elif in_s:
           only_standalone += 1
       elif in_r:
           only_series += 1
       else:
           in_neither += 1

   print(f"  In INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md only: {only_standalone}")
   print(f"  In INSPECTION_LOG.md only: {only_series}")
   print(f"  In BOTH: {in_both}")
   print(f"  In NEITHER: {in_neither}")

   if in_both > 0:
       print(f"\n  Branches in BOTH logs:")
       for b in sorted(confirmed):
           if b in standalone_log and b in series_log:
               print(f"    {b}")

   if in_neither > 0:
       print(f"\n  Branches in NEITHER log:")
       for b in sorted(confirmed):
           if b not in standalone_log and b not in series_log:
               print(f"    {b}")

   print(f"\n=== SERIES CONFIRMED (confirmed_series.txt) ===")
   print(f"Total heads: {len(confirmed_series)}")

   s_only_standalone = 0
   s_only_series = 0
   s_in_both = 0
   s_in_neither = 0

   for b in sorted(confirmed_series):
       in_s = b in standalone_log
       in_r = b in series_log
       if in_s and in_r:

       elif in_s:
           s_only_standalone += 1
       elif in_r:
           s_only_series += 1
       else:
           s_in_neither += 1
       elif in_r:
           s_only_series += 1
       else:
           s_in_neither += 1

   print(f"  In INSPECTION_LOG.md only: {s_only_series}")
   print(f"  In INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md only: {s_only_standalone}")
   print(f"  In INSPECTION_LOG.md only: {s_only_series}")
   print(f"  In INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md only: {s_only_standalone}")
   print(f"  In BOTH: {s_in_both}")
   print(f"  In NEITHER: {s_in_neither}")

  standalone.txt

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import os, re

   # Load all confirmed drops
   confirmed_standalone = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/confirmed.txt'))
   confirmed_series_heads = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/confirmed_series.txt'))
   drops = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/drop_new.txt'))

   # Load all keeps
   standalone_keep = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/standalone.txt'))
   series_keep = {}  # branch -> series head
   for sf in os.listdir('import/series'):
       members = [l.strip() for l in open(f'import/series/{sf}') if l.strip()]
       for m in members:
           series_keep[m] = sf

   # Load log references
   standalone_log = set()
   for line in open('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md'):
       for m in re.finditer(r'\b(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})\b', line):
           standalone_log.add(m.group(1))

   series_log = set()
   for line in open('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md'):
       for m in re.finditer(r'\b(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})\b', line):
           series_log.add(m.group(1))

   all_log = standalone_log | series_log

   print("=== STANDALONE KEEPS (standalone.txt) ===")
   print(f"Total: {len(standalone_keep)}")
   issues = []
   for b in sorted(standalone_keep):
       if b in drops:
           issues.append(f"  ERROR: {b} is also in drop_new.txt!")
       if b not in all_log:
           issues.append(f"  ERROR: {b} has no log entry!")
       if b in confirmed_standalone:
           issues.append(f"  ERROR: {b} is in confirmed.txt (should be keep, not confirmed drop)!")
   if issues:
       for i in issues:
           print(i)
   else:
       print("  All clean: no overlaps with drops, all have log entries, none in confirmed drops.")

❯ Additionally, just for convenience, can you unify the INSPECTION_LOG*md files into one comprehensive file -- groupped by 1) DROPS and KEEPS and 2) by

 Bash command

   # Get counts and lists for structuring
   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re, os

   # Parse both logs for all decisions
   def parse_entries(filename):
       entries = []
       current = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           m = re.match(r'^## (Series: )?(.*)', line)
           if m and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current:
                   entries.append((current, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current = line.strip()
               lines = [line.strip()]
           elif current:
               if line.startswith('## ') and '20' not in line[:20]:
                   if current:
                       entries.append((current, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current = None
                   lines = []
               else:
                   lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current:
           entries.append((current, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
● Bash(# Get counts and lists for structuring
      python3 << 'PYEOF'…)
  ⎿  Series: 47 entries (13 KEEP, 29 DROP)
     Standalone: 194 entries (43 KEEP, 151 DROP)

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re

   def parse_entries(filename):
       entries = []
       current_heading = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           if line.startswith('## ') and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current_heading = line.strip()
               lines = []
           elif line.startswith('# ') and not line.startswith('## '):
               # Skip top-level headings
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current_heading = None
                   lines = []
           elif current_heading:
               lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current_heading:
           entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   def is_keep(heading, body):
       return 'KEEP' in heading

   def is_drop(heading, body):
       if 'DROP' in heading:
           return True
       if 'dissolved' in heading.lower():
           return True
       if '**Decision**: DROP' in body or '**Decision**:' in body and 'DROP' in body:
           return True
       return False

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')

 Bash command

   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re

   def parse_entries(filename):
       """Parse ## headings and their bodies. Each entry = one branch or series."""
       entries = []
       current_heading = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           if line.startswith('## ') and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current_heading = line.strip()
               lines = []
           elif line.startswith('# ') and not line.startswith('## '):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current_heading = None
                   lines = []
           elif current_heading:
               lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current_heading:
           entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   def is_keep(heading, body):
       return 'KEEP' in heading

   def is_drop(heading, body):
       if 'DROP' in heading:
           return True
       if 'dissolved' in heading.lower():
           return True
       return False

   def get_primary_branch(heading):
       """Get the first branch ID from a heading."""
       m = re.search(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', heading)
       return m.group(1) if m else ''

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
   standalone_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')

   # Deduplicate: track which primary branch IDs we've seen
   seen = set()
   def dedup(entries):
       result = []
       for heading, body in entries:
           bid = get_primary_branch(heading)
           if bid and bid not in seen:
               seen.add(bid)
               result.append((heading, body))
           elif bid:
               pass  # skip duplicate
       return result

   # Categorize
   series_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if is_keep(h,b)])
   seen_before_standalone = set(seen)
   standalone_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if is_keep(h,b)])

   seen2 = set()
   series_drop = []
   for h,b in series_entries:
       if is_drop(h,b):
           bid = get_primary_branch(h)
           if bid not in seen2:
               seen2.add(bid)
               series_drop.append((h,b))

   standalone_drop = []
   for h,b in standalone_entries:
       if is_drop(h,b):
           bid = get_primary_branch(h)
           if bid not in seen2:
               seen2.add(bid)
               standalone_drop.append((h,b))

   # Check for entries that are neither KEEP nor DROP
   unclassified_s = [(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if not is_keep(h,b) and not is_drop(h,b)]
   unclassified_a = [(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if not is_keep(h,b) and not is_drop(h,b)]

   print(f"Series KEEP: {len(series_keep)}")
   print(f"Standalone KEEP: {len(standalone_keep)}")
   print(f"Series DROP: {len(series_drop)}")
   print(f"Standalone DROP: {len(standalone_drop)}")
   print(f"Unclassified series: {len(unclassified_s)}")
   print(f"Unclassified standalone: {len(unclassified_a)}")

   if unclassified_s:
       print("\nUnclassified series:")
       for h,b in unclassified_s:
           print(f"  {h[:80]}")

   if unclassified_a:

  - 5 branches appear in both logs by cross-reference text only, not as own entries — not duplicates

────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 Bash command

   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re

   def parse_entries(filename):
       entries = []
       current_heading = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           if line.startswith('## ') and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current_heading = line.strip()
               lines = []
           elif line.startswith('# ') and not line.startswith('## '):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current_heading = None
                   lines = []
           elif current_heading:
               lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current_heading:
           entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   def classify(heading, body):
       if 'KEEP' in heading:
           return 'KEEP'
       if 'DROP' in heading or 'dissolved' in heading.lower():
           return 'DROP'
       # Check body for Decision line
       for line in body.split('\n'):
           if '**Decision**' in line or 'Decision' in line:
               if 'DROP' in line:
                   return 'DROP'
               if 'KEEP' in line:
                   return 'KEEP'
       # Check for "Dropped branches" without explicit Decision
       if '**Dropped branches**' in body and 'KEEP' not in heading:
           return 'DROP'
       # Check for "Already upstream" in all table rows
       if 'Already upstream' in body and 'Not upstream' not in body:
           return 'DROP'
       return 'UNKNOWN'

   def get_primary_branch(heading):
       m = re.search(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', heading)
       return m.group(1) if m else ''

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
   standalone_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')

   # Classify all
   series_keep = []
   series_drop = []
   standalone_keep = []
   standalone_drop = []
   unknown = []

   seen = set()

   for h, b in series_entries:
       bid = get_primary_branch(h)
       if bid in seen:
           continue
       seen.add(bid)
       c = classify(h, b)
       if c == 'KEEP':
           series_keep.append((h, b))
       elif c == 'DROP':
           series_drop.append((h, b))
       else:
           unknown.append(('series', h, b))

   for h, b in standalone_entries:
       bid = get_primary_branch(h)
       if bid in seen:
           continue
       seen.add(bid)
       c = classify(h, b)
       if c == 'KEEP':
           standalone_keep.append((h, b))
       elif c == 'DROP':
           standalone_drop.append((h, b))
       else:
           unknown.append(('standalone', h, b))

   print(f"Series KEEP: {len(series_keep)}")
   print(f"Series DROP: {len(series_drop)}")
   print(f"Standalone KEEP: {len(standalone_keep)}")
   print(f"Standalone DROP: {len(standalone_drop)}")
   print(f"UNKNOWN: {len(unknown)}")

   print(f"Standalone KEEP: {len(standalone_keep)}")
   print(f"Standalone DROP: {len(standalone_drop)}")
   print(f"UNKNOWN: {len(unknown)}")

     Total: 36
       All clean: no overlaps with drops, all have log entries, none in confirmed drops.

 Bash command

   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re, os

   def parse_entries(filename):
       entries = []
       current_heading = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           if line.startswith('## ') and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current_heading = line.strip()
               lines = []
           elif line.startswith('# ') and not line.startswith('## '):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current_heading = None
                   lines = []
           elif current_heading:
               lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current_heading:
           entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   def classify(heading, body):
       if 'KEEP' in heading:
           return 'KEEP'
       if 'DROP' in heading or 'dissolved' in heading.lower():
           return 'DROP'
       for line in body.split('\n'):
           if '**Decision**' in line or 'Decision' in line:
               if 'DROP' in line:
                   return 'DROP'
               if 'KEEP' in line:
                   return 'KEEP'
       if '**Dropped branches**' in body and 'KEEP' not in heading:
           return 'DROP'
       if 'Already upstream' in body and 'Not upstream' not in body:
           return 'DROP'
       return 'UNKNOWN'

   def get_all_branches(heading):
       return re.findall(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', heading)

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
   standalone_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')

   # Dedup by checking if ANY branch in heading is new (not just first)
   seen = set()

   def dedup(entries):
       result = []
       for heading, body in entries:
           branches = get_all_branches(heading)
           if any(b not in seen for b in branches):
               for b in branches:
                   seen.add(b)
               result.append((heading, body))
       return result

   series_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   series_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])

   standalone_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   standalone_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])

   unknown_s = [(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'UNKNOWN']
   unknown_a = [(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'UNKNOWN']

   print(f"Series KEEP: {len(series_keep)}")
   print(f"Series DROP: {len(series_drop)}")
   print(f"Standalone KEEP: {len(standalone_keep)}")
   print(f"Standalone DROP: {len(standalone_drop)}")
   print(f"Unknown: {len(unknown_s) + len(unknown_a)}")
   print(f"Series DROP: {len(series_drop)}")
   print(f"Standalone KEEP: {len(standalone_keep)}")
   print(f"Standalone DROP: {len(standalone_drop)}")

   # Re-run the generation script (same as before)
   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re

   def parse_entries(filename):
       entries = []
       current_heading = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           if line.startswith('## ') and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current_heading = line.strip()
               lines = []
           elif line.startswith('# ') and not line.startswith('## '):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current_heading = None
                   lines = []
           elif current_heading:
               lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current_heading:
           entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   def classify(heading, body):
       if 'KEEP' in heading:
           return 'KEEP'
       if 'DROP' in heading or 'dissolved' in heading.lower():
           return 'DROP'
       for line in body.split('\n'):
           if 'Decision' in line:
               if 'DROP' in line: return 'DROP'
               if 'KEEP' in line: return 'KEEP'
       if '**Dropped branches**' in body and 'KEEP' not in heading:
           return 'DROP'
       if 'Already upstream' in body and 'Not upstream' not in body:
           return 'DROP'
       return 'UNKNOWN'

   seen = set()
   def dedup(entries):
       result = []
       for h, b in entries:
           branches = re.findall(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', h)
           if any(br not in seen for br in branches):
               for br in branches:
                   seen.add(br)
               result.append((h, b))
       return result

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
   standalone_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')

   series_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   series_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])
   standalone_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   standalone_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])

   out = []
   out.append('# Patch Inspection — Unified Log')
   out.append('')
   out.append('Record of every inspected branch with decision and evidence.')
   out.append('Pipeline documentation: [FINAL_REPORT.md](FINAL_REPORT.md).')
   out.append('')
   out.append('---')
   out.append('')
   out.append('## KEEP — Series')
   out.append('')
   out.append(f'{len(series_keep)} series. Series files in [`series/`](series/), overview in [`SERIES.md`](SERIES.md).')
   out.append('')
   for h, b in series_keep:
       out.append(h)
       out.append(b)
       out.append('')
   out.append('---')
   out.append('')
   out.append('## KEEP — Standalone')
   out.append('')
   out.append(f'{len(standalone_keep)} entries. Full list: [`standalone.txt`](standalone.txt).')
   out.append('')
   for h, b in standalone_keep:
       out.append(h)
       out.append(b)
       out.append('')
   out.append('---')
   out.append('')
   out.append('## DROP — Series')
   out.append('')
   out.append(f'{len(series_drop)} series. Confirmed: [`confirmed_series.txt`](confirmed_series.txt).')
   out.append('All dropped branches in [`drop_new.txt`](drop_new.txt).')
   out.append('')
   for h, b in series_drop:
       out.append(h)
       out.append(b)
       out.append('')
   out.append('---')
   out.append('')
   out.append('## DROP — Standalone')
   out.append('')
   out.append(f'{len(standalone_drop)} entries. Confirmed: [`confirmed.txt`](confirmed.txt).')
   out.append('All in [`drop_new.txt`](drop_new.txt).')
   out.append('')
   for h, b in standalone_drop:
       out.append(h)
       out.append(b)
       out.append('')

   with open('import/INSPECTION_LOG_UNIFIED.md', 'w') as f:
       f.write('\n'.join(out))

   # Final verification
   unified_text = '\n'.join(out)
   import os
   standalone_keep_set = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/standalone.txt'))
   series_heads_set = set(os.listdir('import/series'))
   drops_set = set(l.strip() for l in open('import/drop_new.txt'))

   missing_sa = [b for b in sorted(standalone_keep_set) if b not in unified_text]
   missing_sh = [b for b in sorted(series_heads_set) if b not in unified_text]
   missing_dr = [b for b in sorted(drops_set) if b not in unified_text]

   print(f"Series KEEP: {len(series_keep)}, DROP: {len(series_drop)}")
   print(f"Standalone KEEP: {len(standalone_keep)}, DROP: {len(standalone_drop)}")
   print(f"Missing standalone KEEPs: {len(missing_sa)}")
   print(f"Missing series heads: {len(missing_sh)}")
   print(f"Missing drops: {len(missing_dr)}")
   print(f"Lines: {len(out)}")

   if not missing_sa and not missing_sh and not missing_dr:
       print("\nALL BRANCHES PRESENT.")
   else:
       for b in missing_sa: print(f"  missing SA KEEP: {b}")
       for b in missing_sh: print(f"  missing series: {b}")
       for b in missing_dr: print(f"  missing drop: {b}")

      def parse_entries(filename):

❯ But how did it happen? Why was it split in two?

● Looking at the subjects:

  2025-04-0266: [RFC PATCH v2 2/7] i386: Add PSP discovery code        — Alec Brown
  2025-04-0267: [RFC PATCH v2 3/7] slaunch/psp: Add core PSP commands   — Alec Brown
  2025-04-0268: [RFC PATCH v2 4/7] slaunch/psp: Setup TMRs              — Alec Brown
  ---
  2025-04-0270: [RFC PATCH v2 1/7] i386: Extra x86 definitions          — Ross Philipson
  2025-04-0271: [RFC PATCH v2 5/7] slaunch/skinit: AMD SKINIT core      — Ross Philipson
  2025-04-0272: [RFC PATCH v2 6/7] efi: Add AMD SKINIT support          — Ross Philipson

  It's one 7-patch series (RFC PATCH v2, parts 1-7) with two authors. The series grouping script in Phase 1 split it into two because it groups by (author,
  version, part_total, month, proximity) — Brown and Philipson have different author names, so the grouper created two separate series files. Branch
  2025-04-0269 (part 7/7, the missing patch) isn't in failed.txt at all.

  It's actually correct to keep them as two series files — they're co-authored parts of the same submission but from different people. The mistake was only
  in the INSPECTION_LOG where I merged them into one heading for convenience during investigation. That's what I just fixed.

   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re, os

   def parse_entries(filename):
       entries = []
       current_heading = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           if line.startswith('## ') and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current_heading = line.strip()
               lines = []
           elif line.startswith('# ') and not line.startswith('## '):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current_heading = None
                   lines = []
           elif current_heading:
               lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current_heading:
           entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   def classify(heading, body):
       if 'KEEP' in heading: return 'KEEP'
       if 'DROP' in heading or 'dissolved' in heading.lower(): return 'DROP'
       for line in body.split('\n'):
           if 'Decision' in line:
               if 'DROP' in line: return 'DROP'
               if 'KEEP' in line: return 'KEEP'
       if '**Dropped branches**' in body and 'KEEP' not in heading: return 'DROP'
       if 'Already upstream' in body and 'Not upstream' not in body: return 'DROP'
       return 'UNKNOWN'

   seen = set()
   def dedup(entries):
       result = []
       for h, b in entries:
           branches = re.findall(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', h)
           if any(br not in seen for br in branches):
               for br in branches: seen.add(br)
               result.append((h, b))
       return result

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
   standalone_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')

   series_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   series_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])
   standalone_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   standalone_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])

   # Add series/ links to KEEP series headings
   existing_files = set(os.listdir('import/series'))

   out = []
   out.append('# Patch Inspection — Unified Log')
   existing_files = set(os.listdir('import/series'))

   out = []
   out.append('# Patch Inspection — Unified Log')

● Issues found. Let me investigate:

  1. Section 3: 2025-07-0029, 2025-10-0294, 2025-10-0304 — these are KEEP series members that appear in the DROP section because they have individual
  "Already upstream" verdicts in table rows within KEEP series. The unified file's DROP-Series section includes the KEEP series entries that have "Dropped
  branches" lines mentioning these IDs as cross-references. This is a parsing issue — these branch IDs appear in the DROP section text but as evidence, not
  as drop decisions.
  2. Section 4 overlaps: same cause — branch IDs appear as cross-references across sections.
  3. Section 5 duplicate: 2025-06-0121 appears in both standalone log (as KEEP) and again with 2025-06-0143 in a grouped heading.

  The core issue is that the section parser treats ANY branch ID mention as belonging to that section. I need to make the check smarter — only flag branches
  that have their own ## heading in the wrong section, not just cross-references in evidence text.

❯ But how did it happen? Why was it split in two?

● Looking at the subjects:

  2025-04-0266: [RFC PATCH v2 2/7] i386: Add PSP discovery code        — Alec Brown
  2025-04-0267: [RFC PATCH v2 3/7] slaunch/psp: Add core PSP commands   — Alec Brown
  2025-04-0268: [RFC PATCH v2 4/7] slaunch/psp: Setup TMRs              — Alec Brown
  ---
  2025-04-0270: [RFC PATCH v2 1/7] i386: Extra x86 definitions          — Ross Philipson
  2025-04-0271: [RFC PATCH v2 5/7] slaunch/skinit: AMD SKINIT core      — Ross Philipson
  2025-04-0272: [RFC PATCH v2 6/7] efi: Add AMD SKINIT support          — Ross Philipson

  It's one 7-patch series (RFC PATCH v2, parts 1-7) with two authors. The series grouping script in Phase 1 split it into two because it groups by (author,
  version, part_total, month, proximity) — Brown and Philipson have different author names, so the grouper created two separate series files. Branch
  2025-04-0269 (part 7/7, the missing patch) isn't in failed.txt at all.

  It's actually correct to keep them as two series files — they're co-authored parts of the same submission but from different people. The mistake was only
  in the INSPECTION_LOG where I merged them into one heading for convenience during investigation. That's what I just fixed.

● Now to answer the broader question — are there other KEEP branches that should be grouped together? The approach:

  1. For each standalone KEEP, get the target files from FAILED.patch
  2. For each series KEEP, get the target files from all members
  3. Find standalones that touch the same files as a series, or standalones that touch the same files as each other
  4. Cross-check subjects/topics for related work

● Issues found. Let me investigate:

  1. Section 3: 2025-07-0029, 2025-10-0294, 2025-10-0304 — these are KEEP series members that appear in the DROP section because they have individual
  "Already upstream" verdicts in table rows within KEEP series. The unified file's DROP-Series section includes the KEEP series entries that have "Dropped
  branches" lines mentioning these IDs as cross-references. This is a parsing issue — these branch IDs appear in the DROP section text but as evidence, not
  as drop decisions.
  2. Section 4 overlaps: same cause — branch IDs appear as cross-references across sections.
  3. Section 5 duplicate: 2025-06-0121 appears in both standalone log (as KEEP) and again with 2025-06-0143 in a grouped heading.

  The core issue is that the section parser treats ANY branch ID mention as belonging to that section. I need to make the check smarter — only flag branches
  that have their own ## heading in the wrong section, not just cross-references in evidence text.

❯ But how did it happen? Why was it split in two?

● Looking at the subjects:

  2025-04-0266: [RFC PATCH v2 2/7] i386: Add PSP discovery code        — Alec Brown
  2025-04-0267: [RFC PATCH v2 3/7] slaunch/psp: Add core PSP commands   — Alec Brown
  2025-04-0268: [RFC PATCH v2 4/7] slaunch/psp: Setup TMRs              — Alec Brown
  ---
  2025-04-0270: [RFC PATCH v2 1/7] i386: Extra x86 definitions          — Ross Philipson
  2025-04-0271: [RFC PATCH v2 5/7] slaunch/skinit: AMD SKINIT core      — Ross Philipson
  2025-04-0272: [RFC PATCH v2 6/7] efi: Add AMD SKINIT support          — Ross Philipson

  It's one 7-patch series (RFC PATCH v2, parts 1-7) with two authors. The series grouping script in Phase 1 split it into two because it groups by (author,
  version, part_total, month, proximity) — Brown and Philipson have different author names, so the grouper created two separate series files. Branch
  2025-04-0269 (part 7/7, the missing patch) isn't in failed.txt at all.

  It's actually correct to keep them as two series files — they're co-authored parts of the same submission but from different people. The mistake was only
  in the INSPECTION_LOG where I merged them into one heading for convenience during investigation. That's what I just fixed.

 Bash command

   # Regenerate unified log (same script as before)
   python3 << 'PYEOF'
   import re, os

   def parse_entries(filename):
       entries = []
       current_heading = None
       lines = []
       for line in open(filename):
           if line.startswith('## ') and re.search(r'20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4}', line):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
               current_heading = line.strip()
               lines = []
           elif line.startswith('# ') and not line.startswith('## '):
               if current_heading:
                   entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
                   current_heading = None
                   lines = []
           elif current_heading:
               lines.append(line.rstrip())
       if current_heading:
           entries.append((current_heading, '\n'.join(lines)))
       return entries

   def classify(heading, body):
       if 'KEEP' in heading: return 'KEEP'
       if 'DROP' in heading or 'dissolved' in heading.lower(): return 'DROP'
       for line in body.split('\n'):
           if 'Decision' in line:
               if 'DROP' in line: return 'DROP'
               if 'KEEP' in line: return 'KEEP'
       if '**Dropped branches**' in body and 'KEEP' not in heading: return 'DROP'
       if 'Already upstream' in body and 'Not upstream' not in body: return 'DROP'
       return 'UNKNOWN'

   seen = set()
   def dedup(entries):
       result = []
       for h, b in entries:
           branches = re.findall(r'(20\d{2}-\d{2}-\d{4})', h)
           if any(br not in seen for br in branches):
               for br in branches: seen.add(br)
               result.append((h, b))
       return result

   series_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG.md')
   standalone_entries = parse_entries('import/INSPECTION_LOG_STANDALONE.md')

   series_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   series_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in series_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])
   standalone_keep = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'KEEP'])
   standalone_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])

   existing_files = set(os.listdir('import/series'))

   standalone_drop = dedup([(h,b) for h,b in standalone_entries if classify(h,b) == 'DROP'])

   existing_files = set(os.listdir('import/series'))
